# Test Report

Time: 2024-04-17 10:15 PM

### Base Program

```py
def multiplication(x, y):
	result = 0
	while y > 0:
		result += x
		y -= 1
	return result
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def multiplication(x, y):
	result = 0
	while y > 0:
		result += x
		y -= 1
	return result
```

<details>
<summary>interpreter endpoint: passed âœ…</summary>

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def multiplication(x, y):
	result = 0
	while y > 0:
		result += x
		y -= 1
	return result
```

<details>

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def multiplication(x, y):
	result = 0
	while y > 0:
		result += x
		y -= 1
	return result
```

<details>

## Test Case 5

### Modified Program

```py
def multiplication(x, y):
	result = 0
	while y > 0:
		result += x
		y -= 1
	return result
```

## Test Case 6

### Modified Program

```py
def multiplication(x, y):
	result = 0
	while y > 0:
		result += x
		y -= 1
	return result
```

<details>

## Test Case 7

### Modified Program

```py
def multiplication(x, y):
	result = 0
	while y > 0:
		result += x
		y -= 1
	return result
```

<details>

## Test Case 8

### Modified Program

```py
def multiplication(x, y):
	result = 0
	while y > 0:
		result += x
		y -= 1
	return result
```

<details>

## Test Case 9

### Modified Program

```py
def multiplication(x, y):
	result = 0
	while y > 0:
		result += x
		y -= 1
	return result
```
